2018. 3. 8. 22:57, 양우성 : suppose (a/d,b/d)=k k/=1
a/d=kn  b/d=km n,m 서로소
a=dkn b=dkm
(a,b)=dk
contradiction
k=1
r=n s=m
(r,s)=1
